<body class=""><script>  class Page {
    constructor() {

      this.elementId = $('#alm-content div').first().attr('id');

      $('#alm-content').bind('DOMNodeRemoved', (e) => {
        var element = e.target;
        if (element.id == this.elementId && typeof this.onDestroy === 'function') {
          this.onDestroy();
        }
      });

    }
  }</script><script>  class Component {
    constructor(elementId) {
      this._callbacks = {};

      this.elementId = elementId;
      if (this.elementId) {
        $('#' + this.elementId).bind('DOMNodeRemoved', (e) => {
          var element = e.target;
          if (element.id == this.elementId && typeof this.onDestroy === 'function') {
            this.onDestroy();
          }
        });
      }

    }

    addListener(callback, id = this.randomString()) {
      this._callbacks[id] = callback;
      return id;
    }

    removeListener(id) {
      delete this._callbacks[id];
      return true;
    }

    emit(message) {
      const callbacks = this._callbacks || {};
      Object.keys(this._callbacks || {}).forEach((id) => {
        if (typeof callbacks[id] === 'function') {
          callbacks[id](message);
        }
      });
    }

    randomString(len = 6) {
      let charSet = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789';
      let randomString = '';
      for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) {
        let randomPoz = Math.floor(Math.random() * charSet.length);
        randomString += charSet.substring(randomPoz, randomPoz + 1);
      }
      charSet = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz';
      return randomString;
    }
  }</script><div id="alm-before"><div id="ZLNoy7CB3c">

<script>
  (() => {
    class WindowService {
      constructor() { };

      open(url, target='_self') {
        const { device } = window;
        console.log("windows service");
        if (device && device.get('platform') !== 'browser') {
          const target ='_system';
          if (url.includes('authorization')) {
          // Si la URL contiene 'authorization', utiliza window.location.href en IOS tiene que abrirlo en la aplicacion sino no dejan subirla
            // url = url.replace('localhost', ip);
          window.location.href = url;
          } else {
           // Si no contiene 'authorization', utiliza window.open a través de postMessage para el resto de acciones como descargas
           device.postMessage('executeScript', { script: `window.open('${url}', '${target}')` });
          }
        } else {
           // window.location.href = url;
          window.open(url, target);
        }
      }
    }
    window.windowService = new WindowService();
  })()
</script>
<script>
  (() => {
    class CapiService {
      constructor() {};

      checkIfCampaignExist(urlString) {
        const fbclidTokenLogged = this.getCAPIToken(urlString);

        if (!fbclidTokenLogged) {
          return {
            token: '',
            exist: false
          }
        }

        return {
          token: fbclidTokenLogged,
          exist: true
        };
      }

      getCAPIToken(urlString) {
        const url = new URL(urlString);
        const queryParamsObj = {};

        url.searchParams.forEach((value, key) => {
          queryParamsObj[key] = value;
        });

        const fbclidToken = connector.memory().long('fbclid-token');
        const fbclidQueryParams = queryParamsObj.fbclid;

        connector.memory().long('fbclid-token', fbclidQueryParams ? fbclidQueryParams : (fbclidToken || ''));
        return fbclidQueryParams || fbclidToken;
      }

      async sendEventCAPI(object) {
        await connector.ready();

        const capiRes = await connector.http.post('send_capi_event', {
            query: object
          })
          .then((resp) => {
            if (resp) {
              // console.log('Evento CAPI enviado: ', object)
            };
          })
          .catch((err) => {
            console.log(err)
          })
      }
    }
    window.capiService = new CapiService();
  })()
</script>
<script>
  if (typeof TrackingService === 'undefined') {
    class TrackingService {

      async track(object) {

        // Object backup
        const objectOriginal = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(object));

        // Get containerId
        const containerId = object.gtmId || '';
        delete object.gtmId;

        // Get pixelId
        const pixelId = object.pixelId || '';
        delete object.pixelId;

        // iframe flow
        if (typeof window.parentWindow !== 'undefined') {

          if (containerId) {
            window.parentWindow.send({
              key: 'track',
              containerOrPixelId: containerId,
              eventObject: object
            });
          }

          if (pixelId) {
            window.parentWindow.send({
              key: 'track',
              containerOrPixelId: pixelId,
              eventObject: object
            });
          }

          return;
        }

        // const cookies = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('fv_cookies')) || {};
        // if (!cookies.analytics && object.event !== 'Purchase') {
        //   return;
        // }

        // microsite flow
        if (containerId) {
          this.trackEvent(containerId, object);
        }
        if (pixelId) {
          this.trackEvent(pixelId, object);
        }

      }

      getCookiesSettings() {
        return new Promise((resolve) => {

          if (typeof window.parentWindow !== 'undefined') {
            window.parentWindow.receive((data) => {
              if (data.key === 'getCookiesSettings') {
                resolve(data.value);
              }
            });
            window.parentWindow.send({
              key: 'getCookiesSettings'
            });
            return;
          }

          const cookies = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('fv_cookies')) || {};
          resolve(cookies);

        });
      }

      getFBC() {
        return new Promise((resolve) => {

          if (typeof window.parentWindow !== 'undefined') {
            window.parentWindow.receive((data) => {
              if (data.key === 'getFBC') {
                resolve(data.value);
              }
            });
            window.parentWindow.send({
              key: 'getFBC'
            });
            return;
          }

          this.addTrackingService().then(() => {

            if (window.fvTrackingService) {
              resolve(window.fvTrackingService.getFBC());
            } else {
              setTimeout(async () => {
                resolve(await this.getFBC());
              }, 500);
            }

          });
        });
      }

      getFBP() {
        return new Promise((resolve) => {

          if (typeof window.parentWindow !== 'undefined') {
            window.parentWindow.receive((data) => {
              if (data.key === 'getFBP') {
                resolve(data.value);
              }
            });
            window.parentWindow.send({
              key: 'getFBP'
            });
            return;
          }

          this.addTrackingService().then(() => {

            if (window.fvTrackingService) {
              resolve(window.fvTrackingService.getFBP());
            } else {
              setTimeout(async () => {
                resolve(await this.getFBP());
              }, 500);
            }

          });
        });
      }

      getGoogleAdsCookie() {
        return new Promise((resolve) => {

          if (typeof window.parentWindow !== 'undefined') {
            window.parentWindow.receive((data) => {
              if (data.key === 'getGoogleAdsCookie') {
                resolve(data.value);
              }
            });
            window.parentWindow.send({
              key: 'getGoogleAdsCookie'
            });
            return;
          }

          this.addTrackingService().then(() => {

            if (window.fvTrackingService) {
              resolve(window.fvTrackingService.getGoogleAdsCookie());
            } else {
              setTimeout(async () => {
                resolve(await this.getGoogleAdsCookie());
              }, 500);
            }

          });
        });
      }

      async trackEvent(containerOrPixelId, eventObject) {
        await this.addTrackingService();

        if (window.fvTrackingService) {
          window.fvTrackingService.track(containerOrPixelId, eventObject);
        } else {
          setTimeout(async () => {
            this.trackEvent(containerOrPixelId, eventObject);
          }, 500);
        }
      }

      addTrackingService() {
        const isScriptInserted = !!document.getElementById('fv_tracking_service');
        const isScriptLoaded = !!document.getElementById('fv_tracking_service')?.loaded;
        return new Promise(async (resolve, _) => {

          if (isScriptInserted) {
            if (!isScriptLoaded) {
              setTimeout(async () => {
                resolve(this.addTrackingService());
              }, 500);
            } else {
              resolve(true);
            }
            return;
          }

          var script = window.document.createElement("script");
          script.id = 'fv_tracking_service';
          script.src = '/assets/tracking/';
          script.type = "text/javascript";

          if (script.readyState) { // IE
            script.onreadystatechange = () => {
              if (script.readyState == "loaded" || script.readyState == "complete") {
                script.onreadystatechange = null;
                script.loaded = true;
                resolve(true);
              }
            };
          } else { // Others
            script.onload = () => {
              script.loaded = true;
              resolve(true);
            };
          }

          window.document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
        });
      }

    }

    window.trackingService = new TrackingService();
  }
</script>
<script>
  if (typeof HeaderComponent === 'undefined') {
    class HeaderComponent extends Component {

      constructor() {
        super('ZLNoy7CB3c');

        this.title = '';
        this.hideLogo = false;
        this.hideLogoWithoutScroll = false;

        this.lastSection = 'discover';
        this.lastSectionRoute = {};
        this.lastScrollRoute = {};
        this.navigatorObject = window.navigator;
        this.style = 'opaque';
        this.styleWithoutScroll = 'opaque';
        this.arrayRoutes;
        this.init();
      }

      async init() {
        await connector.ready();
        const route = this.getRoute();
        const segments = this.getSegments();

        this.lastSection = connector.memory().short('header/lastSection') || 'discover';
        this.lastSectionRoute = connector.memory().short('header/lastSectionRoute') || {};

        setTimeout(function() {
          $('#telon').fadeOut('slow');
        }, 1);

        if (segments[1] === 'my-tickets') {
          this.setGlobalSection('my-tickets', route);
        } else if (segments[1] === 'my-account') {
          this.setGlobalSection('my-account', route);
        } else {
          this.setGlobalSection('discover', route);
        }

        this.printUnreadMessages();

        this.listenEvents();
        this.controlScroll();
        this.controlKeyboard();
        this.saveFbclidToken();
      }

      saveFbclidToken() {
        const url = new URL(window.location.href);
        const queryParamsObj = {};

        url.searchParams.forEach((value, key) => {
          queryParamsObj[key] = value;
        });

        if (queryParamsObj.fbclid) {
          connector.memory().long('fbclid-token', queryParamsObj.fbclid);
        }
      }

      listenEvents() {
        if (typeof minivents === 'undefined') {
          setTimeout(() => this.listenEvents(), 100);
          return;
        }
        minivents.on('chat/unread-messages', (message) => {
          this.printUnreadMessages();
        });
      }

      printUnreadMessages() {
        const unreadMessages = connector.memory().short('chat/unread-messages') || 0;
        $('#unread-messages').html(unreadMessages);
        if (unreadMessages) {
          $('#unread-messages').show();
        } else {
          $('#unread-messages').hide();
        }
      }

      controlScroll() {
        let headerLastStyle = 'opaque';
        $('body').scroll((e) => {
          const scroll = $('body').scrollTop();
          const title = this.getTitle();
          const backRoute = this.getBackRoute();
          const headerStyle = this.getStyle();
          const route = this.getRoute();
          const lastScrollRoute = this.getLastScrollRoute();

          this.lastScrollRoute[route] = scroll;
          this.setLastScrollRoute(lastScrollRoute);

          if (this.getStyleWithoutScroll() === 'transparent') {
            $('#header-bg').css('transition', '300ms');
            $('#header-bg')
              .removeClass('bg-transparent bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-900 text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 border-b border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800 bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-900 text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 bg-opacity-70 dark:bg-opacity-50 border-0 border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800 border-opacity-70 dark:border-opacity-50');

            if (!scroll) {
              this.setStyle(this.getStyleWithoutScroll(), true);
              if (this.hideLogoWithoutScroll) {
                $('#header #header-back-arrow-and-title').removeClass('flex').hide();
              }
            } else {
              this.setStyle('translucent', true);
              if (this.hideLogoWithoutScroll) {
                $('#header #header-back-arrow-and-title').addClass('flex').show();
              }
            }
          }

        });
      }

      getRoute() {
        let route = document.location.href.substr(10);
        route = route.substr(route.indexOf('/') + 1);
        route = route.substr(route.indexOf('/') + 1);
        return route;
      }

      getSegments() {
        return this.getRoute().split('/');
      }

      setHideLogo(value) {
        this.hideLogo = value;
        this.showBackArrowOrLogo();
        // setTimeout(() => this.showBackArrowOrLogo(), 300);
      }

      setHideLogoWithoutScroll(value) {
        this.hideLogoWithoutScroll = value;
        if (value) {
          $('#header #header-back-arrow-and-title').removeClass('flex').hide();
        } else {
          $('#header #header-back-arrow-and-title').addClass('flex').show();
        }
      }

      controlKeyboard() {
        const isAndroid = window.navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i) !== null;
        const isiOS = window.navigator.userAgent.match(/(iPad)|(iPhone)|(iPod)/i) !== null;
        const isMobile = (isiOS || isAndroid);
        let initialWidth = window.innerWidth;
        let initialHeight = window.innerHeight;
        let tecladoAbierto = false;

        window.onresize = (event) => {
          if (isMobile) {
            if (initialWidth < window.innerWidth) {
              initialWidth = window.innerWidth;
            }
            if (initialHeight < window.innerHeight) {
              initialHeight = window.innerHeight;
            }
            if (initialWidth === window.innerWidth && initialHeight > window.innerHeight + 120) {
              if (!tecladoAbierto) {
                $('#global-sections-mobile').parent().hide();
                $('#footer-reservas-mobile').hide();
                $('#resumen-detalle').parent().hide();
                $('#button-continuar-base').hide();
              }
              tecladoAbierto = true;
            } else if (initialWidth === window.innerWidth && initialHeight <= window.innerHeight + 60) {
              if (tecladoAbierto) {
                $('#global-sections-mobile').parent().show();
                $('#footer-reservas-mobile').show();
                $('#resumen-detalle').parent().show();
                $('#button-continuar-base').show();
              }
              tecladoAbierto = false;
            }
          }
        };
      }

      setTitle(newTitle = '') {
        this.title = newTitle;
        $('#header #header-title').html(this.title);
        if (!this.title) {
          $('#header #header-title').css('display', 'none!important');
        } else {
          $('#header #header-title').addClass('animated fadeIn').css('display', 'flex!important');
        }
        this.showBackArrowOrLogo();
        $('body').scrollTop(this.lastScrollRoute[this.getRoute()] || 0);
      }

      getTitle() {
        return this.title;
      };

      getSegments() {


        let route = document.location.href.substr(10);
        route = route.substr(route.indexOf('/') + 1);
        route = route.substr(route.indexOf('/') + 1);
        return route.split('/');
      };

      setBackRoute(route = '') {
        this.backRoute = route;
        if (!this.backRoute) {
          $('#header #header-back-arrow').removeClass('animated fadeIn flex').css('display', 'none!important');
        } else {
          $('#header #header-back-arrow').addClass('animated fadeIn flex').css('display', 'flex!important');
        }
        this.showBackArrowOrLogo();
      }

      getBackRoute() {
        return this.backRoute;
      };

      setLastSectionRoute(section, route) {
        const segments = this.getSegments();
        const project = segments[0] || '';

        this.setLastSection(section);
        this.lastSectionRoute[project] = this.lastSectionRoute[project] || {};
        if (typeof this.lastSectionRoute[project] === 'string') {
          this.lastSectionRoute[project] = {};
        }

        this.lastSectionRoute[project][section] = route;
        connector.memory().short('header/lastSectionRoute', this.lastSectionRoute);
      }

      getLastSectionRoute(section) {
        const segments = this.getSegments();
        const project = segments[0] || '';

        this.lastSectionRoute = connector.memory().short('header/lastSectionRoute') || {};
        this.lastSectionRoute[project] = this.lastSectionRoute[project] || {};
        if (typeof this.lastSectionRoute[project] === 'string') {
          this.lastSectionRoute[project] = {};
        }
        let lastRoute = this.lastSectionRoute[project][section ? section : this.getLastSection()] || '';
        lastRoute = lastRoute.indexOf('/') === 0 ? lastRoute : '';

        if (this.lastSection === section) {
          lastRoute = '';
        }

        return lastRoute;
      };

      resetSection(section) {
        const segments = this.getSegments();
        const project = segments[0] || '';

        this.lastSectionRoute = connector.memory().short('header/lastSectionRoute') || {};
        this.lastSectionRoute[project] = this.lastSectionRoute[project] || {};
        if (typeof this.lastSectionRoute[project] === 'string') {
          this.lastSectionRoute[project] = {};
        }
        this.lastSectionRoute[project][section] = '';

        connector.memory().short('header/lastSectionRoute', this.lastSectionRoute);
      }

      setLastSection(section) {
        this.lastSection = section;
        connector.memory().short('header/lastSection', this.lastSection);
      }

      getLastSection() {
        return connector.memory().short('header/lastSection') || 'discover';
      };

      setStyle(newStyle, isScroll) {
        this.style = newStyle;
        if (!isScroll) {
          this.styleWithoutScroll = newStyle;
          $('#header-clear').css('display', ['opaque'].includes(newStyle) ? 'block' : 'none');
        }
        this.showBackArrowOrLogo();

        this.setGlobalSection(this.getLastSection() || 'discover', this.getLastSectionRoute() || '', isScroll);
      };

      getStyle() {
        return this.style;
      };

      getStyleWithoutScroll() {
        return this.styleWithoutScroll;
      }

      setLastScrollRoute(newLastScrollRoute) {
        this.lastScrollRoute = newLastScrollRoute;
      };

      getLastScrollRoute() {
        return this.lastScrollRoute;
      };

      setGlobalSection(globalSection, route, isScroll = false) {
        this.setLastSectionRoute(globalSection, route);

        const headerStyle = this.getStyle();

        // Devolvemos los botones del header a su estado normal
        $('#header-bg, #header-mobile-bg')
          .removeClass('bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-900 text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 border-b border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800 bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-900 text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 bg-opacity-70 dark:bg-opacity-50 border-0 border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800 border-opacity-70 dark:border-opacity-50 bg-transparent');
        $('#global-sections-desktop .header-button')
          .removeClass('text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-200 sm:hover:text-black dark:sm:hover:text-white cursor-pointer bg-transparent sm:hover:bg-black dark:sm:hover:bg-white sm:hover:bg-opacity-5 dark:sm:hover:bg-opacity-5 text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-200 sm:hover:text-black dark:sm:hover:text-white cursor-pointer bg-transparent sm:hover:bg-white sm:hover:bg-opacity-10 text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-200 sm:hover:text-black dark:sm:hover:text-white cursor-pointer bg-transparent sm:hover:bg-black dark:sm:hover:bg-white sm:hover:bg-opacity-5 dark:sm:hover:bg-opacity-5 bg-black dark:bg-white bg-opacity-5 dark:bg-opacity-5 text-black dark:text-white bg-black dark:bg-white bg-opacity-5 dark:bg-opacity-5 text-black dark:text-white bg-black dark:bg-white bg-opacity-5 dark:bg-opacity-5 text-black dark:text-white');

        switch (headerStyle) {
          case 'transparent':
            $('#header-bg').addClass('bg-transparent');
            $('#header-mobile-bg').addClass('bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-900 text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 bg-opacity-70 dark:bg-opacity-50 border-0 border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800 border-opacity-70 dark:border-opacity-50');
            $('#global-sections-desktop .header-button')
              .addClass('text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-200 sm:hover:text-black dark:sm:hover:text-white cursor-pointer bg-transparent sm:hover:bg-white sm:hover:bg-opacity-10');
            $('#header-bg').css('backdrop-filter', 'blur(0px)').css('-webkit-backdrop-filter', 'blur(0px)');
            $(' #header-mobile-bg').css('backdrop-filter', 'blur(8px)').css('-webkit-backdrop-filter', 'blur(8px)');
            break;
          case 'translucent':
            $('#header-bg, #header-mobile-bg').addClass('bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-900 text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 bg-opacity-70 dark:bg-opacity-50 border-0 border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800 border-opacity-70 dark:border-opacity-50');
            $('#global-sections-desktop .header-button')
              .addClass('text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-200 sm:hover:text-black dark:sm:hover:text-white cursor-pointer bg-transparent sm:hover:bg-black dark:sm:hover:bg-white sm:hover:bg-opacity-5 dark:sm:hover:bg-opacity-5');
            $('#header-bg, #header-mobile-bg').css('backdrop-filter', 'blur(8px)').css('-webkit-backdrop-filter', 'blur(8px)');
            break;
          default:
            $('#header-bg, #header-mobile-bg').addClass('bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-900 text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 border-b border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800');
            $('#global-sections-desktop .header-button')
              .addClass('text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-200 sm:hover:text-black dark:sm:hover:text-white cursor-pointer bg-transparent sm:hover:bg-black dark:sm:hover:bg-white sm:hover:bg-opacity-5 dark:sm:hover:bg-opacity-5');
            $('#header-bg, #header-mobile-bg').css('backdrop-filter', 'blur(0px)').css('-webkit-backdrop-filter', 'blur(0px)');
            break;
        }

        $('#global-sections-desktop i')
          .removeClass('fas')
          .addClass('far');
        $('#global-sections-mobile i')
          .removeClass('fas')
          .addClass('far');

        if (headerStyle === 'transparent') {
          $('#header-bg').addClass('bg-transparent');
          $('#header-mobile-bg').addClass('bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-900 text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 bg-opacity-70 dark:bg-opacity-50 border-0 border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800 border-opacity-70 dark:border-opacity-50');
          $(`#global-sections-desktop #${globalSection}`)
            .removeClass('text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-200 sm:hover:text-black dark:sm:hover:text-white cursor-pointer bg-transparent sm:hover:bg-white sm:hover:bg-opacity-10')
            .addClass('bg-black dark:bg-white bg-opacity-5 dark:bg-opacity-5 text-black dark:text-white');
          $('#header-bg').css('backdrop-filter', 'blur(0px)').css('-webkit-backdrop-filter', 'blur(0px)');
          $('#header-mobile-bg').css('backdrop-filter', 'blur(8px)').css('-webkit-backdrop-filter', 'blur(8px)');
        } else if (headerStyle === 'translucent') {
          $('#header-bg, #header-mobile-bg').addClass('bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-900 text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 bg-opacity-70 dark:bg-opacity-50 border-0 border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800 border-opacity-70 dark:border-opacity-50');
          $(`#global-sections-desktop #${globalSection}`)
            .removeClass('text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-200 sm:hover:text-black dark:sm:hover:text-white cursor-pointer bg-transparent sm:hover:bg-black dark:sm:hover:bg-white sm:hover:bg-opacity-5 dark:sm:hover:bg-opacity-5')
            .addClass('bg-black dark:bg-white bg-opacity-5 dark:bg-opacity-5 text-black dark:text-white');
          $('#header-bg, #header-mobile-bg').css('backdrop-filter', 'blur(8px)').css('-webkit-backdrop-filter', 'blur(8px)');
        } else {
          $('#header-bg, #header-mobile-bg').addClass('bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-900 text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 border-b border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800');
          $(`#global-sections-desktop #${globalSection}`)
            .removeClass('text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-200 sm:hover:text-black dark:sm:hover:text-white cursor-pointer bg-transparent sm:hover:bg-black dark:sm:hover:bg-white sm:hover:bg-opacity-5 dark:sm:hover:bg-opacity-5')
            .addClass('bg-black dark:bg-white bg-opacity-5 dark:bg-opacity-5 text-black dark:text-white');
          $('#header-bg, #header-mobile-bg').css('backdrop-filter', 'blur(0px)').css('-webkit-backdrop-filter', 'blur(8px)');
        }

        $(`#global-sections-desktop #${globalSection} i`)
          .removeClass('far')
          .addClass('fas');
        $(`#global-sections-mobile #${globalSection} i`)
          .removeClass('far')
          .addClass('fas');

      }

      showBackArrowOrLogo(segments) {
        if (!segments) {
          segments = this.getSegments();
        }

        // if (segments.length > 1) {
        // if (this.hideLogo && segments.length === 1 && !this.backRoute && !this.title) {
        //   $('#header #header-image').css('display', 'none');

        // } else {console.log(this.backRoute, this.title)

        if (this.backRoute || this.title) {

          $('#header #header-image').css('display', 'none');
          $('#header #header-back-arrow-and-title').addClass('flex').css('display', 'flex');

          if (this.backRoute) {
            $('#header #header-back-arrow').addClass('flex').css('display', 'flex');
          } else {
            $('#header #header-back-arrow').removeClass('flex').css('display', 'none');
          }

          if (this.title) {
            $('#header #header-title').addClass('flex').css('display', 'flex');
            if (this.backRoute) {
              $('#header #header-logo').removeClass('flex').css('display', 'none');
            } else {
              $('#header #header-logo').addClass('flex').css('display', 'flex');
            }
          } else {
            $('#header #header-title').removeClass('flex').css('display', 'none');
            $('#header #header-logo').removeClass('flex').css('display', 'none');
          }

        } else {
          $('#header #header-image').css('display', 'flex');
          $('#header #header-back-arrow').removeClass('flex').css('display', 'none');
        }
        // }
      }

      onClickSection(section) {
        const segments = this.getSegments();
        const project = segments[0] || '';

        const rootRoute = (section === 'discover' ? '/' + project : '/' + project +
          '/' + section);
        const lastRoute = this.getLastSectionRoute(section);
        window.navigate(lastRoute || rootRoute);
      }

      onClickChat() {
        chatComponent.toggle();
        return;

        modal.confirm({
          message: `
            <div class="text-center">
              <i class="text-5xl fal fa-info-circle"></i>
              <div class="mt-6 text-xl font-semibold text-black dark:text-white">¿Necesitas ayuda?</div>
              <div class="mt-3">Contacta con soporte@fourvenues.com</div>
            </div>
          `,
          buttons: [{
              text: 'Cerrar',
              class: 'is-light',
              handler: () => {
                modal.close();
              }
            },
            {
              text: 'Contactar',
              class: 'is-primary',
              handler: async () => {
                modal.close();
                window.location.href = 'mailto:soporte@fourvenues.com';
              }
            }
          ]
        });
      }

      onClickBackArrow() {
        if (typeof this.backRoute === 'function') {
          this.backRoute();
        } else if ((this.backRoute || '').indexOf('http') === 0) {
          window.location.href = this.backRoute;
        } else {
          window.navigate(this.backRoute);
        }
      }

      onClickLogoAndTitle() {
        let logo = document.getElementById('header-logo');
        if (logo) {
          if (logo.style.display !== 'none') {
            this.onClickSection('discover');
          }
        }
      }
    }
    window.headerComponent = new HeaderComponent();
  }
</script>

</div><script>
  if (typeof RouterService === 'undefined') {
    class RouterService {
      constructor() {
        const segments = this.getSegments();
        this.backRoute = segments.splice(0, segments.length - 2).join('/');

        const redirect_url = localStorage.getItem('iframe.window.location.href');
        if (redirect_url) {
          localStorage.setItem('iframe.window.location.href', '');
          window.location.href = redirect_url;
        }
      }

      getRoute() {
        let route = document.location.href.substr(10).split('/');
        route = route.splice(route[0] !== 'discover' || route[0] !== 'iframe' ? 2 : 1, route.length).join('/')
        return route;
      }

      getSegments(firstValue = 0, lastValue) {
        return this.getRoute().split('/').splice(firstValue, lastValue === null || lastValue === undefined ? this.getRoute().split('/').length : lastValue);
      }

      setBackRoute(route) {
        this.backRoute = route;
      }

      getBackRoute() {
        const params = this.getSegments(this.getSegments.length - 1)[0];
        const route = params.split('?')[1];

        if(this.backRoute.indexOf('?') !== -1){
          this.backRoute = this.backRoute.split('?')[0];
        }

        return this.backRoute + (route ? `?${route}` : '');
      }

      getParams(segmentsParams = null) {
        let params = {};
        let segments = segmentsParams ? segmentsParams : this.getSegments(this.getSegments.length - 1)[0];

        if(segments.indexOf('?') !== -1 || segments.indexOf('&') !== -1 || segments.indexOf('=') !== -1){
          if (segments.indexOf('?') !== -1) {
            params = segments.split('?')[1]
          }else{
            params = segments;
          }

          if(params.includes('&')){
            params = params.split('&');
          }else{
            params = [params];
          }

          if(params.length !== 0 || Object.keys(params) !== 0){
            params = params.reduce((acc, param) => {
              let [key = '', value = ''] = param.split('=');

              if(value.indexOf(',') !== -1){
                value = value.split(',');
              }

              acc[key] = value;
              return acc;
            }, {});
            return params;
          }
        }

        params = [];
        return params;
      }

      /**
      * @name navigateTo.
      * @param {string} routeLocal - Route a la cual se va navegar.
      * @paramsActual {string} paramsActual - Actual params en url.
      * @description
        * 1. Se recupera la url actual "@routeLocal" con los parametros del usuario y los parametros que se añaden por los componentes
        * 2. Si @routeLocal contiene parametros, se eliminan de @paramsActual para que no se solapen
        * 3. Se crea un array con los parametros de @routeLocal
        * 4. Se recorren los parametros de @routeLocal "@paramsActual" y convierte en un string legible para la url
        * 5. Se redirecciona a la url con los parametros de @routeLocal que contiene los parametros del usuario y los parametros nuevos de la url a la que se va viajar
      * @return {void}
      * @example
      * navigateTo('gengis-kan/events?event=1&services=tickets,guest-list');
      */

      navigateTo(routeLocal){
        const params = this.getSegments(this.getSegments.length - 1)[0];
        let paramsActual = params.split('?')[1];

        if(routeLocal.indexOf('?') !== -1){
          const routeLocalParams = this.getParams(routeLocal);
          const arrParamsLocal = Object.keys(routeLocalParams);

          const routeParams = this.getParams(paramsActual);
          arrParamsLocal.forEach(param => {
            if(routeParams[param]){
              delete routeParams[param];
              paramsActual = routeParams;
            }
          });

          paramsActual = Object.keys(routeParams).reduce((acc, param, i) => {
            if(Object.keys(routeParams).length > 1){
              acc += `${param}=${routeParams[param]}${i !== (Object.keys(routeParams).length - 1) ? '&' : ''}`;
            }
            else{
              acc += `${param}=${routeParams[param]}`;
            }
            return acc;
          }, '');

          navigate(`${routeLocal}&${paramsActual}`);
          return;
        }

        paramsActual = paramsActual ? `?${paramsActual}` : '';
        navigate(`${routeLocal}${paramsActual}`);
      }

    }
    window.routerService = new RouterService();
  }
</script>
<script>
  if (typeof ListadoEventosComponent === 'undefined') {
    class ListadoEventosComponent extends Component {
      constructor() {
        super();
        this.init();
      }

      async init() {
        await $l.script('/libs/moment.min.js');
        if (typeof(moment) !== 'undefined') {
          moment.locale('es');
        }
      }

      onClickEvent(evento_slug, evento_codigo, microsite_slug, evento_name, evento_date) {
        this.emit({
          evento_codigo: evento_codigo,
          evento_slug: evento_slug,
          microsite_slug: microsite_slug
        });

        window.trackEvent('select_content', {
          content_name: evento_name || 'N/A',
          content_date: this.epochToFormatedDate(evento_date ?? 0)
        });
      }

       // I had to create again this function here because I was not be able
       // to call the function from tools.php or tools.js
      epochToFormatedDate(epochTime) {
        const date = new Date(epochTime * 1000);

        const year = date.getUTCFullYear();
        const month = ('0' + (date.getUTCMonth() + 1)).slice(-2);
        const day = ('0' + date.getUTCDate()).slice(-2);
        const hours = ('0' + date.getUTCHours()).slice(-2);
        const minutes = ('0' + date.getUTCMinutes()).slice(-2);

        return `${year}-${month}-${day} ${hours}:${minutes}`;
      }

      showAllEvents(){

        let year = '';
        let month = '';

        const eighthEventEpoch = null;
        // If the 8º event exists we have to navigate to the 8º event date month page
        if(eighthEventEpoch) {
          const nextEventDate = moment.unix(eighthEventEpoch).format("YYYY-MM-DD");
          year = nextEventDate.split('-')[0];
          month =  nextEventDate.split('-')[1];
        } else {
          year = moment().format('YYYY-MM-DD').split('-')[0];
          month =  moment().format('YYYY-MM-DD').split('-')[1];
        }

        let date = year + '-' + month;

        if('' !== '1'){
          navigate(`/luminata-disco/events?date=${date}`);
          return;
        }
        routerService.navigateTo(`/iframe/luminata-disco/events?date=${date}`);
      }
    }
    window.listadoEventosComponent = new ListadoEventosComponent();
  };
</script>

  (() => {
    class CapiService {
      constructor() {};

      checkIfCampaignExist(urlString) {
        const fbclidTokenLogged = this.getCAPIToken(urlString);

        if (!fbclidTokenLogged) {
          return {
            token: '',
            exist: false
          }
        }

        return {
          token: fbclidTokenLogged,
          exist: true
        };
      }

      getCAPIToken(urlString) {
        const url = new URL(urlString);
        const queryParamsObj = {};

        url.searchParams.forEach((value, key) => {
          queryParamsObj[key] = value;
        });

        const fbclidToken = connector.memory().long('fbclid-token');
        const fbclidQueryParams = queryParamsObj.fbclid;

        connector.memory().long('fbclid-token', fbclidQueryParams ? fbclidQueryParams : (fbclidToken || ''));
        return fbclidQueryParams || fbclidToken;
      }

      async sendEventCAPI(object) {
        await connector.ready();

        const capiRes = await connector.http.post('send_capi_event', {
            query: object
          })
          .then((resp) => {
            if (resp) {
              // console.log('Evento CAPI enviado: ', object)
            };
          })
          .catch((err) => {
            console.log(err)
          })
      }
    }
    window.capiService = new CapiService();
  })()
</script>

  if (typeof CookiesComponent === 'undefined') {
    class CookiesComponent extends Component {

      constructor() {
        super('x7KpxcAQ10');
        this.init();
      }

      init() {
        const cookies = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('fv_cookies')) || {};
        console.log(cookies);
        if (!cookies.hideCookies) {
          this.showCookies();
        }
        this.manageCookiesIcons();
      }

      showCookies() {
        document.getElementById('cookies-message').style.display = 'block';
      }

      manageCookiesIcons() {
        const cookies = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('fv_cookies')) || {};
        if (cookies.analytics) {
          document.getElementById('footer-cookies-icon').className = 'far fa-check-circle';
          document.getElementById('cookies-check').className = 'fas fa-check-circle text-xl text-blue-500';
        } else {
          document.getElementById('footer-cookies-icon').className = 'far fa-exclamation-triangle';
          document.getElementById('cookies-check').className = 'far fa-circle text-xl text-gray-400';
        }
      }

      onClickAcceptCookies() {
        const cookies = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('fv_cookies')) || {};
        cookies.hideCookies = true;
        cookies.analytics = true;
        localStorage.setItem('fv_cookies', JSON.stringify(cookies));
        document.getElementById('cookies-message').style.display = 'none';
        this.manageCookiesIcons();
      }

      onClickManageCookies() {
        document.getElementById('cookies-message').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('cookies-manage').style.display = 'block';
      }

      onClickAnalyticsCookies() {
        if (document.getElementById('cookies-check').classList.contains('fa-check-circle')) {
          document.getElementById('cookies-check').className = 'far fa-circle text-xl text-gray-400';
        } else {
          document.getElementById('cookies-check').className = 'fas fa-check-circle text-xl text-blue-500';
        }
      }

      onClickSaveCookies() {
        const cookies = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('fv_cookies')) || {};
        cookies.hideCookies = true;
        cookies.analytics = document.getElementById('cookies-check').classList.contains('fa-check-circle');
        localStorage.setItem('fv_cookies', JSON.stringify(cookies));
        document.getElementById('cookies-manage').style.display = 'none';
        this.manageCookiesIcons();
      }

    }
    window.cookiesComponent = new CookiesComponent();
  }
</script>

<script>
  function Events(target) {
    var events = {},
      empty = [];
    target = target || this;
    target.on = function (type, func, ctx) {
      (events[type] = events[type] || []).push([func, ctx]);
      return target
    };
    target.off = function (type, func) {
      type || (events = {});
      var list = events[type] || empty,
        i = list.length = func ? list.length : 0;
      while (i--) func == list[i][0] && list.splice(i, 1);
      return target
    };
    target.emit = function (type) {
      var e = events[type] || empty,
        list = e.length > 0 ? e.slice(0, e.length) : e,
        i = 0,
        j;
      while (j = list[i++]) j[0].apply(j[1], empty.slice.call(arguments, 1));
      return target
    }
  }
</script>

<script>
  function getDeviceInfo() {
    const device = {};

    if (window.matchMedia('(max-width: 639px)').matches) {
      device.type = 'small';
      device.size = 0;
    }
    if (window.matchMedia('(min-width: 640px)').matches) {
      device.type = 'mobile';
      device.size = 1;
    }
    if (window.matchMedia('(min-width: 768px)').matches) {
      device.type = 'tablet';
      device.size = 2;
    }
    if (window.matchMedia('(min-width: 1024px)').matches) {
      device.type = 'desktop';
      device.size = 3;
    }
    if (window.matchMedia('(min-width: 1280px)').matches) {
      device.type = 'widescreen';
      device.size = 4;
    }
    if (window.matchMedia('(min-width: 1536px)').matches) {
      device.type = 'fullhd';
      device.size = 5;
    }

    const iOS = /iPad|iPhone|iPod/.test(navigator.userAgent) && !window.MSStream;

    // Get the device pixel ratio
    const ratio = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;

    // Define the users device screen dimensions
    const screen = {
      width: window.screen.width * ratio,
      height: window.screen.height * ratio
    };

    // iPhone X Detection
    if (iOS && (
      (screen.width === 1125 && screen.height === 2436) ||
      (screen.width === 828 && screen.height === 1792)
    )) {
      device.iphoneX = true;
    }

    device.iOS = iOS;
    device.ratio = ratio;
    device.width = screen.width;
    device.height = screen.height;

    device.webview = /(iPhone|iPod|iPad).*AppleWebKit(?!.*Safari)/i.test(navigator.userAgent);

    device.isInWebAppiOS = (window.navigator.standalone === true);
    device.isInWebAppChrome = (window.matchMedia('(display-mode: standalone)').matches);

    const standalone = device.standalone = device.isInWebAppiOS || device.isInWebAppChrome;

    const userAgent = window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
    const safari = device.safari = /safari/.test(userAgent);
    const ios = /iphone|ipod|ipad/.test(userAgent);

    if (ios) {
      if (!standalone && safari) {
        device.browser = true;
      } else if (standalone && !safari) {
        device.standalone = true;
      } else if (!standalone && !safari) {
        device.uiwebview = true;
      }
    } else {
      device.iOS = false;
    }

    return device;
  }
</script>

<script>
  window.minivents = new Events();
  window.onPopStateSections = ['content', 'js'];
  window.previousPageIsModal = false;
  window.firstPageViewSent = false;
  window.externalId = Date.now().toString();

  window.navigate = (route) => {
    const url = "https://cli.fourvenues.com";
    const isRedirectNewMicrosites = false;
    const isRedirectOLDMicrosites = false;
    const domain = "https://www.fourvenues.com";
    const urlWWW = "https://www.fourvenues.com";

    const lang = "/es";
    route = route || '';
    const segments = (route.indexOf('/') === 0 ? route.substr(1) : route).split('/');

    // Mostramos el loader si existe en la página actual
    $('#contenido').hide();
    $('#cargando').show();
    previousPageIsModal = !!$('#modal-page').length;

    // Mostrarmos el logo en el encabezado o la flecha para volver atrás
    // headerComponent.setHideLogo(false);
    headerComponent.setHideLogoWithoutScroll(false);

    if (segments[1] === 'my-tickets') {
      headerComponent.setGlobalSection('my-tickets', route);
    } else if (segments[1] === 'my-account') {
      headerComponent.setGlobalSection('my-account', route);
    } else {
      headerComponent.setGlobalSection('discover', route);
    }

    window.navigateHook(route, segments);

    let isfeatureFlagEnabled = isRedirectNewMicrosites;

    const EVENT_URL = 'events'
    const CALENDAR_URL = 'calendar@'
    const isOrganizationMicrositePage = segments.length == 1;
    const isCalendarPage = segments[1]?.includes(CALENDAR_URL) && segments[2] != undefined;
    const isEventMicrositePage = (segments[1] === EVENT_URL) && segments[2] != '' && segments[3] == undefined;


    const hasRedirectNewCLI = (isOrganizationMicrositePage || isEventMicrositePage || isCalendarPage) && isfeatureFlagEnabled;
    const hasredirectOldCLI = (isOrganizationMicrositePage || isEventMicrositePage || isCalendarPage) && !isRedirectOLDMicrosites;


    //TODO: Cuando la aplicación este lo más estable, se debera cambiar para no tener esta lógica
    //LA FUNCIÓN DE ESTA LÓGICA ES PARA PODER NAVEGAR ENTRES LAS DISTINTOS DOMINIOS. WEB, WWW Y CLI.
    
    //SI MI DOMINIO ACTUAL ES WEB ENTRO
    if (domain === 'http://localhost:8001' || domain === 'https://web-alpha.fourvenues.com' || domain === 'https://web.fourvenues.com') {
      //SI TENGO ACTIVADA LA FF DE REDIRIGIR TODO A LOS ANTIGUOS MICROSITES, SIGO NAVEGANDO DESDE WEB
      if (isRedirectOLDMicrosites) {
        captain.navigate(route, ['content', 'js']);
      } else {
        //SI NO ES ASI MIRO SI ES UNA DE LAS 3 PAGINAS QUE ESTA EN LOS NUEVOS MICROSITES Y DEPENDE SI ES CALENDARIO O NO NAVEGO
        if (hasredirectOldCLI && isCalendarPage) {
          const segments = route.split('/');

          segments[2] = EVENT_URL

          const newRoute = segments.join('/');

          window.location.href = url + lang + newRoute;

          return;
        }
        if (hasredirectOldCLI) {
          const redirectUrl = urlWWW + lang + route;
          window.location.href = redirectUrl

          return;
        }

        captain.navigate(route, ['content', 'js']);
      }
      //SI NO ESTOY EN WEB Y SI QUE ESTOY EN WWW SIGNIFICA QUE SEGUIMOS CON LAS ESTRATEGIA DE SOLO REDIRIGIR A LOS QUE TIENEN LAS NUEVAS MICROSITES ACTIVADAS
    } else {

      if (hasRedirectNewCLI && isCalendarPage) {
        const segments = route.split('/');

        segments[2] = EVENT_URL

        const newRoute = segments.join('/');

        window.location.href = url + lang + newRoute;

        return;
      }

      if (hasRedirectNewCLI) {
        const redirectUrl = url + lang + route;
        window.location.href = redirectUrl

        return;
      }

      captain.navigate(route, ['content', 'js']);
    }
  }

  window.addEventListener('hashchange', this.handleNavigation);

  window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', this.handleNavigation);


  function handleNavigation() {
    const route = '/' + window.location.pathname.split('/').slice(2).join('/');
    const segments = (route.indexOf('/') === 0 ? route.substr(1) : route).split('/');

    if (typeof window.navigateHook === 'function') {
      window.navigateHook(route, segments);
    } else {
      console.warn('window.navigateHook is not defined yet');
    }
  }


  // Aquí puedes ejecutar tu código cuando cambia la ruta
  window.navigateHook = (route, segments) => {

    if (window.parentWindow) {
      window.parentWindow.send({
        key: 'navigate',
        route: route,
        segments: segments
      });
    }
    window.trackRoute(route, segments);
  }

  // Track route
  window.trackRoute = async (route, segments) => {
    await connector.ready();

    if (!route || !segments) {
      route = '/' + window.location.pathname.split('/').slice(2).join('/');
      segments = (route.indexOf('/') === 0 ? route.substr(1) : route).split('/');
    }

    const customParams = {
      route: route
    }
    window.trackEvent('page_view', customParams);
  };


  window.trackEvent = async (eventName, customParams) => {
    await connector.ready();

    const getParentUrl = () => {
      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        if (window.parentWindow) {
          window.parentWindow?.receive((message) => {
            if (message.key === 'currentUrl') {
              return resolve(message.url);
            }
          });
          window.parentWindow?.send({
            key: 'currentUrl'
          });
        } else {
          return resolve(window.location.href);
        }
      });
    }

    const UpdatedEventName = {
      PURCHASE: 'purchase',
      ADD_TO_CART: 'add_to_cart',
      BEGIN_CHECKOUT: 'begin_checkout',
      VIEW_CONTENT: 'view_content',
      PAGE_VIEW: 'page_view',
      SELECT_CONTENT: 'select_content',
      SELECT_ITEM: 'select_item',
      UNSUSCRIBE: 'unsuscribe'
    }

    const emitTrackingEvent = async (eventName, customParams) => {

      const currentUrl = await getParentUrl();
      const campaign = window.capiService?.checkIfCampaignExist(currentUrl);
      const organizationId = 'Lktn6wp3300x801f538qx1k6cBlpGXPD';

      let trackingUniqueID = '';

      //TODO: Verificar si esta comprobación sigue siendo necesaria
      if (eventName === 'purchase') {
        trackingUniqueID = connector.md5(customParams.purchase_id);
        delete customParams.purchase_id;
      } else {
        trackingUniqueID = connector.uniqueId();
      }

      if (organizationId || eventName === UpdatedEventName.UNSUSCRIBE) {

        external_id = connector.md5(`${eventName}${organizationId}${Date.now()}`);

        const [nameValue, emailValue, phoneValue] = [
          getLocalStorageItem('field-name') || getLocalStorageItem('field-nombre'),
          getLocalStorageItem('field-email'),
          getLocalStorageItem('field-telephone') || getLocalStorageItem('field-telefono')
        ];


        window.userEmail = emailValue;
        window.userName = nameValue;
        window.userPhone = phoneValue;

        const results = await Promise.allSettled([
          window.trackingService?.getCookiesSettings() || {},
          window.trackingService?.getFBC() || '',
          window.trackingService?.getFBP() || '',
          window.trackingService?.getGoogleAdsCookie() || ''
        ]);


        const [fvCookies, fbc, fbp, googleAdsCookie] = results.map(result => {
          if (result.status === 'fulfilled') {
            return result.value === null ? '' : result.value;
          } else {
            return '';
          }
        });

        if (fvCookies?.analytics === false) {
          return;
        }

        const trackingObject = {
          event: eventName,
          eventID: trackingUniqueID,
          organization_id: organizationId,
          url_page: currentUrl,
          fbclid: campaign.token || '',
          gcl_cookie: googleAdsCookie,
          fbc,
          fbp,
          user_name: nameValue,
          user_email: emailValue,
          user_phone: phoneValue,
          ...customParams
        };


        const trackingObjectGoogle = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(trackingObject));
        delete trackingObjectGoogle.evento_id;
        delete trackingObjectGoogle.tickets;

        // Sending Google Events...
        generateGTMEcommerceFormatEvent(trackingObjectGoogle);

        const trackingObjectOldGoogle = updateTrackingEventWithOldGTMName(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(trackingObjectGoogle)));

        //Emitimos también el evento de google con los nombres antiguos
        emitGoogleEvent(trackingObjectOldGoogle);

        // Preparing everything before send Pixel / CAPI events...
        const trackingObjectPixel = updateTrackingEventWithOldName(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(trackingObject)));
        delete trackingObjectPixel.gcl_cookie;

        //Hago una copia para trackingObjectCAPI antes de eliminar el array de tickets
        let trackingObjectCAPI = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(trackingObjectPixel));
        delete trackingObjectPixel.tickets;

        const excludedEvents = ['SelectContent', 'select_content', 'view_item', 'SelectItem', 'purchase', 'Purchase'];

        if (!excludedEvents.includes(trackingObjectPixel.event)) {

          switch (trackingObjectCAPI.event) {
            case 'PageView':
            case 'ViewContent':
              trackingObjectCAPI.event_name = trackingObjectCAPI.event;
              trackingObjectCAPI.event_id = trackingObjectCAPI.eventID;
              delete trackingObjectCAPI.event;
              delete trackingObjectCAPI.eventID;
              break;
            case 'AddToCart':
              trackingObjectCAPI = updateAddtoCartCAPIEvent(trackingObjectCAPI);
              break;
            case 'InitiateCheckout':
              trackingObjectCAPI = updateInitiateCheckoutCAPIEvent(trackingObjectCAPI);
              break;
            default:
              break;
          }

          if (trackingObjectPixel.event !== 'Purchase' && trackingObjectPixel.event !== 'Unsuscribe') {

            if (!window.firstPageViewSent || trackingObjectPixel.event !== 'PageView') {

              // We don't have to send user information as custom params in Pixel
              delete trackingObjectPixel.user_name;
              delete trackingObjectPixel.user_email;
              delete trackingObjectPixel.user_phone;

              emitPixelEvent(trackingObjectPixel);
            }

            window.firstPageViewSent = true;

            emitCAPIEvent(trackingObjectCAPI);
          }

        }
      }
    }


    const createSelectContentEcommerceFormatEvent = (trackingObject) => {
      return {
        event: UpdatedEventName.SELECT_CONTENT,
        ecommerce: {
          items: [{
            item_category3: trackingObject.content_name || '',
            item_category4: trackingObject.content_date || '',
            index: 0
          }]
        }
      }
    }

    const createViewContentEcommerceFormatEvent = (trackingObject) => {
      return {
        event: UpdatedEventName.VIEW_CONTENT,
        ecommerce: {
          items: [{
            item_category3: trackingObject.content_name || '',
            item_category4: trackingObject.content_date || '',
            index: 0
          }]
        }
      }
    }



    const createSelectItemEcommerceFormatEvent = (trackingObject) => {
      return {
        event: UpdatedEventName.SELECT_ITEM,
        ecommerce: {
          items: [{
            item_name: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_name,
            item_id: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_id,
            price: trackingObject.items[0]?.price,
            item_category: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_category,
            item_category2: connector.memory().short('pricing-option-name') || '',
            item_category3: trackingObject.content_name || '',
            item_category4: trackingObject.content_date || '',
            item_list_name: mapperSections[trackingObject.items[0]?.item_category] || '',
            quantity: 1,
            index: 0
          }]
        }
      };
    }

    const createAddToCartEcommerceFormatEvent = (trackingObject) => {

      const itemsArray = [{
        item_name: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_name,
        item_id: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_id,
        price: trackingObject.items[0]?.price,
        item_category: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_category,
        item_category2: connector.memory().short('pricing-option-name') || '',
        item_category3: trackingObject.content_name || '',
        item_category4: trackingObject.content_date || '',
        item_list_name: mapperSections[trackingObject.items[0]?.item_category] || '',
        quantity: trackingObject.items[0]?.quantity,
        index: 0
      }];

      return {
        event: UpdatedEventName.ADD_TO_CART,
        ecommerce: {
          currency: trackingObject.currency,
          value: trackingObject.value.toFixed(2),
          items: itemsArray
        }
      }

    }

    const createBeginCheckoutEcommerceFormatEvent = (trackingObject) => {

      let currentItemIndex = 0;

      let itemsArray = [{
        item_name: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_name,
        item_id: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_id,
        price: trackingObject.items[0]?.price,
        item_category: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_category,
        item_category2: connector.memory().short('pricing-option-name') || '',
        item_category3: trackingObject.content_name || '',
        item_category4: trackingObject.content_date || '',
        coupon: trackingObject.items[0]?.coupon,
        discount: trackingObject.items[0]?.discount,
        item_list_name: mapperSections[trackingObject.items[0]?.item_category] || '',
        quantity: trackingObject.items[0]?.quantity,
        index: currentItemIndex
      }];

      currentItemIndex += 1;
      /* I do this verification again because the user can activate this option in the previous page
      and disable it before begin checkout, and viceversa */

      const warrantyInfo = connector.memory().short('warranty-info');

      const isWarrantyEnabled = getParamFromStringUrl(trackingObject.url_page, 'warranty');

      if (warrantyInfo?.warranty && isWarrantyEnabled === 'true') {
        itemsArray.push(getWarrantyArrayItem(trackingObject, warrantyInfo.warranty, currentItemIndex));
        currentItemIndex += 1;
      }

      const complements = connector.memory().short('selected-complements');

      if (complements) {

        const groupedComplements = getComplementArrayItem(trackingObject, complements, currentItemIndex);

        itemsArray = [...itemsArray, ...groupedComplements];
      }

      return {
        event: UpdatedEventName.BEGIN_CHECKOUT,
        ecommerce: {
          currency: trackingObject.currency,
          value: trackingObject.value.toFixed(2),
          subscription: trackingObject.subscription,
          items: itemsArray
        }
      };

    }

    const createPurchaseEcommerceFormatEvent = (trackingObject) => {

      let itemsArray = [{
        item_name: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_name,
        item_id: trackingObject.items[0]?.ticket_id,
        price: trackingObject.items[0]?.price,
        item_category: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_category,
        item_category2: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_option_name || '',
        item_category3: trackingObject.content_name || '',
        item_category4: trackingObject.content_date || '',
        coupon: trackingObject.items[0]?.coupon,
        discount: trackingObject.items[0]?.discount,
        item_list_name: mapperSections[trackingObject.items[0]?.item_category] || '',
        quantity: trackingObject.items[0]?.quantity,
        index: 0

      }];


      if (trackingObject.warrantyInfo) {
        itemsArray.push(trackingObject.warrantyInfo);
      }


      if (trackingObject.groupedComplements) {
        itemsArray = [...itemsArray, ...trackingObject.groupedComplements];
      }

      return {
        event: UpdatedEventName.PURCHASE,
        ecommerce: {
          transaction_id: trackingObject.transaction_id,
          value: trackingObject.value.toFixed(2),
          tax: trackingObject.tax,
          currency: trackingObject.currency,
          coupon: trackingObject.coupon,
          subscription: trackingObject.subscription,
          items: itemsArray
        }
      };
    }

    const eventHandlers = {
      select_content: createSelectContentEcommerceFormatEvent,
      view_content: createViewContentEcommerceFormatEvent,
      select_item: createSelectItemEcommerceFormatEvent,
      add_to_cart: createAddToCartEcommerceFormatEvent,
      begin_checkout: createBeginCheckoutEcommerceFormatEvent,
      purchase: createPurchaseEcommerceFormatEvent
    };


    const mapperSections = {
      "Ticket": "Entradas",
      "List": "Listas",
      "Booking": "Mesas"
    };

    const eventMapper = {
      'page_view': 'PageView',
      'add_to_cart': 'AddToCart',
      'begin_checkout': 'InitiateCheckout',
      'view_content': 'ViewContent',
      'purchase': 'Purchase',
      'select_content': 'SelectContent',
      'select_item': 'SelectItem'
    };

    const eventGTMMapper = {
      'page_view': 'page_view',
      'add_to_cart': 'add_to_cart',
      'begin_checkout': 'begin_checkout',
      'view_content': 'view_content',
      'purchase': 'purchase',
      'select_content': 'select_content',
      'select_item': 'select_item'
    };

    getComplementArrayItem = (trackingObject, complements, currentItemIndex) => {

      const groupedComplements = {};
      let currentComplementsIndex = currentItemIndex;

      Object.values(complements).flat().forEach(complement => {
        const { label, price } = complement;

        if (groupedComplements[label]) {

          groupedComplements[label].quantity += 1;

        } else {

          groupedComplements[label] = {
            item_id: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_id,
            item_name: label,
            price: price,
            item_category: "complement",
            item_category2: connector.memory().short('pricing-option-name') || '',
            item_category3: trackingObject.content_name || '',
            item_category4: trackingObject.content_date || '',
            item_list_name: mapperSections[trackingObject.items[0]?.item_category] || '',
            quantity: 1,
            index: currentComplementsIndex
          };

          currentComplementsIndex += 1;
        }
      });

      return Object.values(groupedComplements);

    }

    const updateTrackingEventWithOldName = (trackingObject) => {
      const mappedEvent = eventMapper[trackingObject.event];

      if (mappedEvent) {
        return {
          ...trackingObject,
          event: mappedEvent
        };
      }

      return { ...trackingObject };
    }

    const updateTrackingEventWithOldGTMName = (trackingObject) => {
      const mappedEvent = eventGTMMapper[trackingObject.event];

      if (eventGTMMapper) {
        return {
          ...trackingObject,
          event: mappedEvent
        };
      }

      return { ...trackingObject };
    }

    const getWarrantyArrayItem = (trackingObject, warrantyObject, currentItemIndex) => {

      return {
        item_name: "Cancelación gratuita",
        item_id: trackingObject.items[0]?.item_id,
        price: connector.memory().short('warranty-subtotal'),
        item_category: 'free cancelation',
        item_category2: connector.memory().short('pricing-option-name') || '',
        item_category3: trackingObject.content_name || '',
        item_category4: trackingObject.content_date || '',
        item_list_name: mapperSections[trackingObject.items[0]?.item_category] || '',
        quantity: trackingObject.items[0]?.quantity,
        index: currentItemIndex

      }
    }

    const generateGTMEcommerceFormatEvent = (trackingObject) => {

      const eventHandler = eventHandlers[trackingObject.event];

      let dataLayerObject = null;

      if (eventHandler) {
        dataLayerObject = eventHandler(trackingObject);
        dataLayerObject.ecommerce.fbc = trackingObject.fbc;
        dataLayerObject.ecommerce.fbp = trackingObject.fbp;
        dataLayerObject.ecommerce.fbclid = trackingObject.fbclid;
        dataLayerObject.ecommerce.url_page = trackingObject.url_page;
        dataLayerObject.ecommerce.eventID = trackingObject.eventID;
        dataLayerObject.ecommerce.organization_id = trackingObject.organization_id;
        dataLayerObject.ecommerce.user_email = trackingObject.user_email || '';
        dataLayerObject.ecommerce.user_phone = trackingObject.user_phone || '';
        dataLayerObject.ecommerce.user_name = trackingObject.user_name || '';
        emitGoogleEvent(dataLayerObject);
      }

    }

    const getParamFromStringUrl = (stringUrl, param) => {
      //
      const regex = new RegExp(`[?&]${param}=([^&#]*)`);
      let match = stringUrl.match(regex);
      return match ? decodeURIComponent(match[1]) : 'false';
    }




    const getLocalStorageItem = (key) => {
      const value = localStorage.getItem(key);
      return value ? value : null;
    }

    const shouldEmitAddToCartEvent = (itemId, itemQuantity) => {
      const savedCart = connector.memory().short('saved-cart');
      if (!savedCart) {
        connector.memory().short('saved-cart', { 'itemId': itemId, 'itemQuantity': itemQuantity });
        return true;
      }

      if (savedCart.itemId !== itemId || (savedCart.itemId === itemId && savedCart.itemQuantity !== itemQuantity)) {
        connector.memory().short('saved-cart', { 'itemId': itemId, 'itemQuantity': itemQuantity });
        return true;
      }

      return false;
    }

    const updateInitiateCheckoutCAPIEvent = (trackingObjectCAPI) => {

      delete trackingObjectCAPI.content_name;

      // Rename some of the parameters before send to CAPI service
      const {
        event: event_name,
        eventID: event_id,
        items: contents,
        items_category: content_type,
        items_name: content_name,
        customer_email: user_email,
        customer_phone: user_phone,
        customer_name: user_name,
        ...otherProperties
      } = trackingObjectCAPI;

      const updatedTrackingObjectCAPI = {
        ...otherProperties,
        event_name,
        event_id,
        contents,
        content_type,
        user_email,
        user_phone,
        user_name,
        content_name
      };

      updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.content_id = updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents && updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents[0].item_id;
      updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.price = updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents && updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents[0].price;
      updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.content_ids = updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents && updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents.map((item) => item.item_id);
      updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.num_items = updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents && updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents.length;

      // Remove useless parameters
      delete updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.customer_email;
      delete updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.customer_phone;
      delete updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.customer_name;
      delete updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.content_date;

      // Update contents parameters names
      let updatedContents = updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents.map(item =>
        ({ item_price: item.price, quantity: item.quantity, id: item.item_id })
      );

      updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents = updatedContents;

      return updatedTrackingObjectCAPI;

    }

    const updateAddtoCartCAPIEvent = (trackingObjectCAPI) => {

      delete trackingObjectCAPI.content_name;

      // Rename some of the parameters before send to CAPI service
      const {
        event: event_name,
        items: contents,
        items_category: content_type,
        items_name: content_name,
        eventID: event_id,
        ...otherProperties
      } = trackingObjectCAPI;

      const updatedTrackingObjectCAPI = {
        ...otherProperties,
        event_name,
        event_id,
        contents,
        content_type,
        content_name
      };

      updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.content_id = updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents && updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents[0].item_id;
      updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.price = updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents && updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents[0].price;
      updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.content_ids = updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents && updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents.map((item) => item.item_id);
      updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.num_items = updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents && updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents.length;


      // Update contents parameters names
      let updatedContents = updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents.map(item =>
        ({ item_price: item.price, quantity: item.quantity, id: item.item_id })
      );

      updatedTrackingObjectCAPI.contents = updatedContents;

      return updatedTrackingObjectCAPI;

    }

    const emitGoogleEvent = (trackingObject) => {
      trackingObject.gtmId = '';
      window.trackingService?.track(trackingObject);

    }


    const emitPixelEvent = (trackingObject) => {
      trackingObject.pixelId = '';
      window.trackingService?.track(trackingObject);
    }

    const emitCAPIEvent = async (trackingObject) => {
      const capiObject = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(trackingObject));
      // CAPI's external_id must be hashed manually
      capiObject.external_id = await connector.sha256(window.externalId);
      window.capiService?.sendEventCAPI(capiObject);
    }

    emitTrackingEvent(eventName, customParams);
  }

  window.getPricingOptionName = (priceId, pricingOptionsString) => {

    if (!pricingOptionsString || !priceId) {
      return '';
    }

    let pricingOptions;

    try {
      pricingOptions = JSON.parse(pricingOptionsString);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error parsing JSON:', error);
      return '';
    }

    const option = pricingOptions.find(option => option._id === priceId);

    if (option && option.hasOwnProperty('name')) {
      return option.name;
    } else {
      return '';
    }

  }

  window.trackInternalGTMEvent = async (eventName, customParams) => {

    const emitInternalGTMTrackingEvent = async (eventName, customParams) => {

      const trackingObject = {
        event: eventName,
        ...customParams
      };

      /* We don't use environment variables in this project
      It will be fixed in new CLI
      */
      trackingObject.pixelId = 'GTM-NRKJ53SH';
      window.trackingService?.track(trackingObject);
    }

    emitInternalGTMTrackingEvent(eventName, customParams);
  }

</script><div id="DY4xOpDFeE"><div id="global-modal">

  <div id="modal-confirmar" class="modal">

    <div class="modal-section animated w-full z-30 my-3 rounded-lg" style="max-width:350px;overflow-y: auto;">
      <div class="box text-center p-0">
        <div style="clear:both;height:1rem;"></div>
        <div id="modal-confirmar-content" class="content text-center p-3"></div>
        <div id="modal-confirmar-buttons"
        class="flex items-center gap-3 mt-6 p-3 sticky w-full dark:bg-gray-700 dark:bg-opacity-60 border-t dark:border-gray-600"
        style="bottom:0px;backdrop-filter:blur(8px);-webkit-backdrop-filter:blur(8px);">
      </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <button class="modal-close is-large" aria-label="close" onclick="modal.cerrar();return false;"></button>
  </div>

  <div id="modal-error" class="modal">
    <div class="modal-background" onclick="modal.cerrar(null, true);return false;" ></div>
    <div class="modal-section animated w-full z-10 my-3 rounded-lg" style="max-width:350px;overflow-y: auto;">
      <div class="box text-center">
        <i class="fal fa-exclamation-triangle text-5xl text-danger dark:text-white"></i>
        <div style="clear:both;height:1rem;"></div>
        <div id="modal-error-content" class="content text-center"></div>
        <div id="modal-error-buttons" class="flex items-center gap-3 mt-6"
        style="bottom:-1px;backdrop-filter:blur(8px);-webkit-backdrop-filter:blur(8px);"></div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <button class="modal-close is-large" aria-label="close" onclick="modal.cerrar();return false;"></button>
  </div>

</div><script type="text/javascript">
  var modal = (function(window, undefined) {
    const public = {};
    const private = {};

    let buttons = [];
    public.blockClose = false;

    const confirm = public.confirm = function(data) {
      const id = 'modal-confirmar';

      public.blockClose = data.blockClose;

      let buttonsHTML = '';
      buttons = (data.buttons || []);
      if ((data.buttons || []).length) {
        $('#' + id + ' #modal-confirmar-buttons').css('opacity', '1');
        for (let b = 0, len = data.buttons.length; b < len; b++) {
          let button = data.buttons[b];
          data.buttons[b].id = b;
          buttonsHTML += '<button class="button flex-1 ' + (button.class || (b ? 'is-primary' : 'is-white')) + '" onclick="modal.buttonClick(' + b + ');return false">' + (button.text || button.label) + '</button>'
        }
        $('#' + id + ' #modal-confirmar-buttons').html(buttonsHTML);
      } else {
        $('#' + id + ' #modal-confirmar-buttons').css('opacity', '0');
      }
      $('#' + id + ' #modal-confirmar-content.content').html(data.message || '');
      open(id);
    }

    const error = public.error = function(data) {
      if (typeof data === 'string') {
        data = {
          message: data
        };
      }
      let html = '<p>' + (data.message || '<b>Error</b>') + '</p>';
      const id = 'modal-error';
      let buttonsHTML = '';
      buttons = (data.buttons || []);
      if ((data.buttons || []).length) {
        for (let b = 0, len = data.buttons.length; b < len; b++) {
          let button = data.buttons[b];
          data.buttons[b].id = b;
          buttonsHTML += '<button class="button flex-1 ' + (button.class || (b ? 'is-primary' : 'is-white')) + '" onclick="modal.buttonClick(' + b + ');return false">' + (button.text || button.label) + '</button>'
        }
      }
      $('#' + id + ' #modal-error-content.content').html(html);
      $('#' + id + ' #modal-error-buttons').html(buttonsHTML);
      open(id);
    }

    const buttonClick = public.buttonClick = function(b) {
      if (buttons[b] && buttons[b].handler && typeof buttons[b].handler === 'function') {
        buttons[b].handler(buttons[b]);
      } else {
        modal.cerrar('modal-confirmar');
        modal.cerrar('modal-error');
      }
    }

    const open = public.open = function(id) {
      if (!id) {
        id = $(event.target).parents('.modal').attr('id');
      }
      $('#' + id + ' .modal-background').fadeIn();
      $('#' + id + ' .modal-card').removeClass('fadeOutDownBig').addClass('fadeInUpBig');
      $('#' + id + ' .modal-content').removeClass('zoomOut').show().addClass('zoomIn');
      $('#' + id + ' .modal-section').removeClass('zoomOut').addClass('zoomIn');
      $('#' + id).addClass('is-active');
    }

    const close = public.close = function(id, isBG) {
      return new Promise((resolve) => {
        if (public.blockClose && isBG) {
          resolve(false);
          return;
        }
        public.blockClose = false;
        if (!id && event && event.target) {
          id = $(event.target).parents('.modal').attr('id');
        }
        if (!id) {
          id = 'modal-confirmar';
        }
        $('#' + id + ' .modal-background').fadeOut();
        $('#' + id + ' .modal-card').removeClass('fadeInUpBig').addClass('fadeOutDownBig');
        $('#' + id + ' .modal-content').removeClass('zoomIn').addClass('zoomOut');
        $('#' + id + ' .modal-section').removeClass('zoomIn').addClass('zoomOut');
        setTimeout(() => {
          $('#' + id).removeClass('is-active');
          resolve(true);
        }, 300);
        if (typeof chat !== 'undefined' && typeof chat.show === 'function') {
          chat.show();
        }
      });
    }

    const scrollOff = public.scrollOff = function() {
      $('#alm-content').css('overflow-y', 'hidden');
    }

    const scrollOn = public.scrollOn = function() {
      $('#alm-content').css('overflow-y', 'auto');
    }

    // Retrocompatibilidad
    const confirmar = public.confirmar = function(data) {
      confirm(data)
    }
    const abrir = public.abrir = function(id) {
      open(id)
    }
    const cerrar = public.cerrar = function(id, isBG) {
      close(id, isBG)
    }

    return public;

  })(window)
</script>

<script>
  if (typeof ChatComponent === 'undefined') {
    class ChatComponent extends Component {

      constructor() {
        super();
        this.isLoaded = false;
        this.isOpened = false;
        this.iframe;
        window.botpress.on('webchat:opened', (conversationId) => {
          this.isOpened = true;
        });

        window.botpress.on('webchat:closed', () => {
          this.isOpened = false;
        });

        window.botpress.on('message', (message) => {
          setUnreadMessages(1);
        });
      }

      async openWidget() {
        $('#chat i')
          .removeClass('far fa-paper-plane')
          .addClass('fad fa-spinner-third fa-spin');

        window.botpress.open();

        this.isLoaded = true;

        setTimeout(() => {
          $('#chat i')
            .removeClass('fad fa-spinner-third fa-spin')
            .addClass('far fa-paper-plane');
        }, 1000);
      }

      setUnreadMessages(currentUnreadMessages) {
        this.unreadCount = currentUnreadMessages;
        connector.memory().short('chat/unread-messages', this.unreadCount);
        minivents.emit('chat/unread-messages', {
          key: 'unread-messages',
          unreadCount: payload.unreadCount
        });
      }

      toggle() {
        if (this.isOpened) {
          this.close();
        } else {
          this.open();
        }
      }

      open() {
        this.openWidget();
      }

      close() {
        window.botpress.close();
      }
    }
    window.chatComponent = new ChatComponent();
  }
</script>
