window.onpopstate = function(event) {
  const route = document.location.href;
  captain.navigate(route, window.onPopStateSections, true);
}
window.captain = (function() {
  const navigate = function(route, sections = [], fromPopState = false) {
    new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
      const firstSlash = route.replace('https://', 'http://').replace('http://', '').indexOf('/');
      route = route.replace('https://', 'http://').replace('http://', '').substr(firstSlash);
      route = '/es' + route.replace('/es/', '/');
      const path = route;
      const almresponse = !sections.length ? 'body' : sections.join(',');
      if ((route || '').indexOf('?') > 0) {
        route += '&almresponse=' + almresponse;
      } else {
        route += '?almresponse=' + almresponse;
      }
      $.ajax(route)
        .done(function(response) {

          if (!fromPopState) {
            window.history.pushState("", "", path);
          }

          const html = $.parseHTML(response, null, true);
          $.each(html, function(i, el) {

            if (el.id === 'alm-before') {
              if (!$('body #alm-before').length) {
                $('body').prepend('<div id="alm-before"></div>');
              }
              $('body #alm-before').html(el.innerHTML);
            }

            if (el.id === 'alm-content') {
              if (!$('body #alm-content').length) {
                if ($('body #alm-before').length) {
                  $('body #alm-before').after('<div id="alm-content"></div>');
                } else {
                  $('body').prepend('<div id="alm-content"></div>');
                }
              }
              $('body #alm-content').html(el.innerHTML);
            }

            if (el.id === 'alm-after') {
              if (!$('body #alm-after').length) {
                if ($('body #alm-content').length) {
                  $('body #alm-content').after('<div id="alm-after"></div>');
                } else if ($('body #alm-before').length) {
                  $('body #alm-before').after('<div id="alm-after"></div>');
                } else {
                  $('body').prepend('<div id="alm-after"></div>');
                }
              }
              $('body #alm-after').html(el.innerHTML);
            }

            if (el.id === 'alm-js') {
              if (!$('body #alm-js').length) {
                if ($('body #alm-after').length) {
                  $('body #alm-after').after('<div id="alm-js"></div>');
                } else if ($('body #alm-content').length) {
                  $('body #alm-content').after('<div id="alm-js"></div>');
                } else if ($('body #alm-before').length) {
                  $('body #alm-before').after('<div id="alm-js"></div>');
                } else {
                  $('body').prepend('<div id="alm-js"></div>');
                }
              }
              $('body #alm-js').html(el.innerHTML);
            }

          });
          resolve("success");
        })
        .fail(function() {
          reject("error");
        });
    });
  }
  return {
    navigate
  }
})();</script><div id="alm-js"><script>

          calendarNavigateComponent.addListener((message) => this.onEmitCalendarNavigateComponent(message));

          listadoEventosComponent.addListener(message => this.onEmitListadoEventosComponent(message));

        await galleryService.prepare();
        galleryService.init('carta', {
          plugins: [lgThumbnail, lgZoom],
          mode: 'fade',
          download: true,
          zoom: true
        });
      }

      initAccordion() {
        $('.read-more').on('click', function() {
          if ($(this).hasClass('collapsed')) {
            $('.info').removeClass('h-11').addClass('h-full');
            $(this).removeClass('collapsed').addClass('rotate-180');
          } else {
            $(this).removeClass('rotate-180').addClass('collapsed');
            $('.info').removeClass('h-full').addClass('h-11');
          }
        });
      }

      async onEmitCalendarComponent(message) {
        if (message && !message.isClosed) {
          const year_month = message.year_month;
          const day = message.day;
          connector.memory().short('day-origin', '');
          navigate(`/luminata-disco/calendar/${year_month}/${day}/bookings`);
        }

      }

      pastEvent() {
        if ('' === 'past_event') {
          modal.error({
            message: '<b>El evento al que estás intentando acceder ya ha terminado.</b>.',
            buttons: [{
              text: 'Cerrar',
              class: 'is-light',
              handler: () => {
                modal.close();
              }
            }]
          });
        }
      }

      onEmitCalendarNavigateComponent(message) {
        if (message && !message.isClosed) {
          navigate(`/luminata-disco/calendar/${message.year}-${message.month}`);
        }
      }

      onEmitListadoEventosComponent(message) {
        connector.memory().short('event-origin', '');
        navigate(`/luminata-disco/events/${message.evento_slug}-${message.evento_codigo}`)
      }

    }

<script>
const clickrefId = 'clickref';

function createCookieClickref(value){
  const d = new Date();
  d.setTime(d.getTime() + (2_592_000_000));

  const expires = "expires="+ d.toUTCString();
  document.cookie = `${clickrefId}=${value};${expires};path=/`;
}

function saveClickref(){
  const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);

  if(urlParams.has(clickrefId)){
    const clickref = urlParams.get(clickrefId);
    createCookieClickref(clickref);
  }
}

saveClickref();

</script>
